--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/combat/burrow_behavior.gd ---
class_name BurrowBehavior
extends Node

"""Periodically burrows underground, becoming
invisible and invulnerable.

Cycles between surface and burrowed states.
Disables Killzone while underground. The entity
can optionally move while burrowed (ambush
pattern).

Useful for worms, moles, or any digging creature.
"""

enum State { SURFACE, BURROWING, UNDERGROUND, EMERGING }

signal burrowed()
signal emerged()

@export var surface_time: float = 4.0
@export var underground_time: float = 2.0
@export var burrow_duration: float = 0.3
@export var emerge_duration: float = 0.3
@export var move_while_burrowed: bool = false
@export var burrow_speed: float = 40.0

var _parent: Node2D
var _state: State = State.SURFACE
var _timer: float = 0.0
var _killzone: Node = null
var _paused: bool = false
var _player: Node2D


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"BurrowBehavior parent must be Node2D"
	)
	_killzone = _parent.get_node_or_null(
		"Killzone"
	)
	_timer = surface_time


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return

	_timer -= delta

	match _state:
		State.SURFACE:
			if _timer <= 0.0:
				_start_burrow()
		State.UNDERGROUND:
			if move_while_burrowed:
				_move_underground(delta)
			if _timer <= 0.0:
				_start_emerge()


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func is_underground() -> bool:
	return _state in [
		State.BURROWING,
		State.UNDERGROUND,
	]


func _start_burrow() -> void:
	_state = State.BURROWING
	_set_killzone_active(false)

	var tween: Tween = _parent.create_tween()
	tween.set_parallel(true)
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "scale:y",
		0.01, burrow_duration,
	).set_ease(Tween.EASE_IN)
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "modulate:a",
		0.2, burrow_duration,
	)
	tween.chain().tween_callback(
		_finish_burrow
	)


func _finish_burrow() -> void:
	_state = State.UNDERGROUND
	_timer = underground_time
	_parent.visible = false
	burrowed.emit()


func _start_emerge() -> void:
	_state = State.EMERGING
	_parent.visible = true

	var tween: Tween = _parent.create_tween()
	tween.set_parallel(true)
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "scale:y",
		1.0, emerge_duration,
	).set_ease(Tween.EASE_OUT)
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "modulate:a",
		1.0, emerge_duration,
	)
	tween.chain().tween_callback(
		_finish_emerge
	)


func _finish_emerge() -> void:
	_state = State.SURFACE
	_timer = surface_time
	_set_killzone_active(true)
	emerged.emit()


func _move_underground(delta: float) -> void:
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		return
	var dir: Vector2 = (
		_player.global_position
		- _parent.global_position
	).normalized()
	_parent.position += (
		dir * burrow_speed * delta
	)


func _set_killzone_active(
	active: bool,
) -> void:
	if not _killzone:
		return
	if _killzone is Area2D:
		_killzone.monitoring = active
		_killzone.monitorable = active
	for child: Node in _killzone.get_children():
		if child is CollisionShape2D:
			child.disabled = not active


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			"player"
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/combat/dash_attack.gd ---
class_name DashAttack
extends Node

"""Charges at the player with a telegraphed dash.

When the player enters trigger_range, the entity
pauses briefly (telegraph phase with flashing),
then dashes at high speed toward the player's
last known position. After the dash, enters a
recovery cooldown.

Pairs well with PatrolMovement or static entities
that need a burst-attack pattern.
"""

enum State {
	IDLE,
	TELEGRAPH,
	DASHING,
	RECOVERING,
}

signal telegraph_started()
signal dash_started()
signal dash_ended()

const GROUP_PLAYER: String = "player"

@export var trigger_range: float = 100.0
@export var dash_speed: float = 400.0
@export var dash_duration: float = 0.3
@export var telegraph_time: float = 0.6
@export var recovery_time: float = 2.0
@export var flash_count: int = 3
@export var flash_color: Color = Color.RED

var _parent: Node2D
var _player: Node2D
var _state: State = State.IDLE
var _timer: float = 0.0
var _dash_dir: Vector2 = Vector2.ZERO
var _dash_elapsed: float = 0.0
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"DashAttack parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return

	match _state:
		State.IDLE:
			_process_idle()
		State.TELEGRAPH:
			_process_telegraph(delta)
		State.DASHING:
			_process_dash(delta)
		State.RECOVERING:
			_process_recovery(delta)


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func is_dashing() -> bool:
	return _state == State.DASHING


func _process_idle() -> void:
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		return
	var dist: float = (
		_parent.global_position.distance_to(
			_player.global_position
		)
	)
	if dist <= trigger_range:
		_start_telegraph()


func _start_telegraph() -> void:
	_state = State.TELEGRAPH
	_timer = telegraph_time
	telegraph_started.emit()
	_play_flash()


func _process_telegraph(delta: float) -> void:
	_timer -= delta
	if _timer <= 0.0:
		_start_dash()


func _start_dash() -> void:
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		_state = State.IDLE
		return

	_dash_dir = (
		_player.global_position
		- _parent.global_position
	).normalized()
	_dash_elapsed = 0.0
	_state = State.DASHING
	_parent.modulate = Color.WHITE
	dash_started.emit()

	_flip_toward(_dash_dir.x)


func _process_dash(delta: float) -> void:
	_dash_elapsed += delta
	if _dash_elapsed >= dash_duration:
		_end_dash()
		return
	_parent.position += (
		_dash_dir * dash_speed * delta
	)


func _end_dash() -> void:
	_state = State.RECOVERING
	_timer = recovery_time
	dash_ended.emit()


func _process_recovery(delta: float) -> void:
	_timer -= delta
	if _timer <= 0.0:
		_state = State.IDLE


func _play_flash() -> void:
	var tween: Tween = _parent.create_tween()
	for i: int in flash_count:
		tween.tween_property(
			_parent, "modulate",
			flash_color,
			telegraph_time / (flash_count * 2.0),
		)
		tween.tween_property(
			_parent, "modulate",
			Color.WHITE,
			telegraph_time / (flash_count * 2.0),
		)


func _flip_toward(dir_x: float) -> void:
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if sprite and abs(dir_x) > 0.01:
		sprite.flip_h = dir_x < 0.0


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			GROUP_PLAYER
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/combat/mimic_behavior.gd ---
class_name MimicBehavior
extends Node

"""Disguises the entity as a harmless object.

While disguised the entity plays a static animation
and its Killzone is disabled. When the player enters
reveal_range, the entity reveals itself: plays the
reveal animation, re-enables the Killzone, and
can start chasing or patrolling.

Useful for surprise monsters: a coin that's actually
a slime, a chest that attacks, etc.
"""

enum State { HIDDEN, REVEALING, REVEALED }

signal revealed()
signal disguised()

const GROUP_PLAYER: String = "player"

@export var disguise_animation: String = "disguise"
@export var reveal_animation: String = "reveal"
@export var idle_animation: String = "default"
@export var reveal_range: float = 50.0
@export var reveal_duration: float = 0.5
@export var can_re_disguise: bool = false
@export var re_disguise_range: float = 200.0

var _parent: Node2D
var _player: Node2D
var _state: State = State.HIDDEN
var _killzone: Node = null
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"MimicBehavior parent must be Node2D"
	)
	_killzone = _parent.get_node_or_null(
		"Killzone"
	)
	_enter_disguise()


func _process(_delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		return

	var dist: float = (
		_parent.global_position.distance_to(
			_player.global_position
		)
	)

	match _state:
		State.HIDDEN:
			if dist <= reveal_range:
				_do_reveal()
		State.REVEALED:
			if (
				can_re_disguise
				and dist > re_disguise_range
			):
				_enter_disguise()


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func is_revealed() -> bool:
	return _state == State.REVEALED


func _enter_disguise() -> void:
	_state = State.HIDDEN
	_set_killzone_active(false)
	_play_anim(disguise_animation)
	disguised.emit()


func _do_reveal() -> void:
	_state = State.REVEALING
	_play_anim(reveal_animation)

	var tween: Tween = _parent.create_tween()
	tween.tween_interval(reveal_duration)
	tween.tween_callback(_finish_reveal)


func _finish_reveal() -> void:
	_state = State.REVEALED
	_set_killzone_active(true)
	_play_anim(idle_animation)
	revealed.emit()


func _set_killzone_active(active: bool) -> void:
	if not _killzone:
		return
	if _killzone is Area2D:
		_killzone.monitoring = active
		_killzone.monitorable = active
	for child: Node in _killzone.get_children():
		if child is CollisionShape2D:
			child.disabled = not active


func _play_anim(anim_name: String) -> void:
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if not sprite:
		return
	if not sprite.sprite_frames:
		return
	if sprite.sprite_frames.has_animation(
		anim_name
	):
		sprite.play(anim_name)


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			GROUP_PLAYER
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/ecosystem/entity_spawner.gd ---
class_name EntitySpawner
extends Node2D

"""Periodically spawns new entities around the parent.

Instantiates a PackedScene at random positions within
a configurable radius. Respects a maximum alive count
and tracks living children to avoid overpopulation.

Spawned entities appear with a small pop-in tween.
"""

signal entity_spawned(entity: Node2D)
signal max_reached()

const POP_SCALE_FROM: float = 0.01
const POP_DURATION: float = 0.3

@export var entity_scene: PackedScene
@export var spawn_interval: float = 5.0
@export var max_alive: int = 4
@export var spawn_radius: float = 40.0
@export var add_to_group: String = ""
@export var spawn_on_ready: bool = true
@export var initial_count: int = 0

var _timer: Timer
var _living: Array[Node2D] = []
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_timer = Timer.new()
	_timer.wait_time = spawn_interval
	_timer.one_shot = false
	_timer.timeout.connect(_on_timer_timeout)
	add_child(_timer)

	if initial_count > 0:
		_spawn_batch(initial_count)

	if spawn_on_ready:
		_timer.start()


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true
	_timer.stop()


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false
	_timer.start()


func get_living_count() -> int:
	_prune_dead()
	return _living.size()


func spawn_one() -> Node2D:
	"""Manually trigger a single spawn.

	Returns:
		The spawned entity, or null if at max or
		no scene assigned.
	"""
	return _try_spawn()


func _on_timer_timeout() -> void:
	if _paused:
		return
	_try_spawn()


func _try_spawn() -> Node2D:
	if not entity_scene:
		return null

	_prune_dead()
	if _living.size() >= max_alive:
		max_reached.emit()
		return null

	var parent: Node2D = get_parent() as Node2D
	if not parent:
		return null

	var entity: Node2D = (
		entity_scene.instantiate() as Node2D
	)
	if not entity:
		return null

	var offset: Vector2 = _random_offset()
	var scene_root: Node = (
		parent.get_tree().current_scene
	)
	scene_root.add_child(entity)
	entity.global_position = (
		parent.global_position + offset
	)

	if add_to_group != "":
		entity.add_to_group(add_to_group)

	_living.append(entity)
	_animate_pop_in(entity)
	entity_spawned.emit(entity)

	return entity


func _spawn_batch(count: int) -> void:
	for i: int in count:
		_try_spawn()


func _prune_dead() -> void:
	"""Remove freed instances from tracking."""
	_living = _living.filter(
		func(e: Node2D) -> bool:
			return is_instance_valid(e)
	)


func _random_offset() -> Vector2:
	var angle: float = randf() * TAU
	var dist: float = randf() * spawn_radius
	return Vector2(
		cos(angle) * dist,
		sin(angle) * dist,
	)


func _animate_pop_in(entity: Node2D) -> void:
	entity.scale = (
		Vector2.ONE * POP_SCALE_FROM
	)
	var tween: Tween = entity.create_tween()
	tween.tween_property(
		entity,
		"scale",
		Vector2.ONE,
		POP_DURATION,
	).set_ease(
		Tween.EASE_OUT
	).set_trans(Tween.TRANS_BACK)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/ecosystem/mutation_behavior.gd ---
class_name MutationBehavior
extends Node

"""Transforms the parent entity into another scene.

Mutation can be triggered by:
- Timer (after X seconds alive).
- Player proximity (within range for Y seconds).
- Low ally count (last survivor evolves).
- Manual call to mutate().

The old entity is removed and replaced by the
mutated scene at the same position. If the old
entity had an ItemDropper, it does NOT drop items
on mutation (only on death).

Plays a brief scale-pulse + color flash on the
entity before swapping.
"""

enum Trigger {
	TIMER,
	PLAYER_PROXIMITY,
	LAST_SURVIVOR,
	MANUAL,
}

signal mutation_started()
signal mutation_complete(new_entity: Node2D)

const FLASH_DURATION: float = 0.4
const PULSE_SCALE: float = 1.4
const GROUP_PLAYER: String = "player"

@export var mutated_scene: PackedScene
@export var trigger: Trigger = Trigger.TIMER
@export var timer_duration: float = 15.0
@export var proximity_range: float = 80.0
@export var proximity_time: float = 3.0
@export var ally_group: String = ""
@export var min_ally_count: int = 1
@export var add_mutated_to_group: String = ""
@export var mutation_color: Color = Color.RED

var _parent: Node2D
var _player: Node2D
var _elapsed: float = 0.0
var _prox_elapsed: float = 0.0
var _mutating: bool = false
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"MutationBehavior parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused or _mutating:
		return

	match trigger:
		Trigger.TIMER:
			_process_timer(delta)
		Trigger.PLAYER_PROXIMITY:
			_process_proximity(delta)
		Trigger.LAST_SURVIVOR:
			_process_survivor()
		Trigger.MANUAL:
			pass


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func mutate() -> void:
	"""Force-trigger the mutation immediately."""
	if _mutating or not mutated_scene:
		return
	_mutating = true
	mutation_started.emit()
	_play_flash_then_swap()


func _process_timer(delta: float) -> void:
	_elapsed += delta
	if _elapsed >= timer_duration:
		mutate()


func _process_proximity(delta: float) -> void:
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		_prox_elapsed = 0.0
		return

	var dist: float = (
		_parent.global_position.distance_to(
			_player.global_position
		)
	)
	if dist <= proximity_range:
		_prox_elapsed += delta
		if _prox_elapsed >= proximity_time:
			mutate()
	else:
		_prox_elapsed = 0.0


func _process_survivor() -> void:
	if ally_group == "":
		return
	var allies: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			ally_group
		)
	)
	var alive: int = 0
	for a: Node in allies:
		if a != _parent and is_instance_valid(a):
			alive += 1
	if alive < min_ally_count:
		mutate()


func _play_flash_then_swap() -> void:
	var tween: Tween = _parent.create_tween()
	tween.set_parallel(true)
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "scale",
		Vector2.ONE * PULSE_SCALE,
		FLASH_DURATION * 0.5,
	).set_ease(Tween.EASE_OUT)
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "modulate",
		mutation_color,
		FLASH_DURATION * 0.5,
	)
	tween.chain().tween_callback(_swap)


func _swap() -> void:
	var pos: Vector2 = _parent.global_position
	var scene_root: Node = (
		_parent.get_tree().current_scene
	)
	var entity: Node2D = (
		mutated_scene.instantiate() as Node2D
	)
	if not entity:
		return

	scene_root.add_child(entity)
	entity.global_position = pos

	if add_mutated_to_group != "":
		entity.add_to_group(
			add_mutated_to_group
		)

	mutation_complete.emit(entity)
	_parent.queue_free()


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			GROUP_PLAYER
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/ecosystem/pack_buff.gd ---
class_name PackBuff
extends Node

"""Buffs the entity when allies are nearby.

Counts nearby entities in the same group and applies
speed/scale multipliers. More allies = stronger buff.
Visual feedback: subtle pulsing glow when buffed.

Useful for swarm enemies that become dangerous in
groups but easy to pick off alone.
"""

signal buff_changed(
	ally_count: int, multiplier: float,
)

const CHECK_INTERVAL: float = 0.5

@export var ally_group: String = "pack"
@export var detection_range: float = 120.0
@export var speed_bonus_per_ally: float = 0.15
@export var max_speed_multiplier: float = 2.0
@export var scale_per_ally: float = 0.05
@export var max_scale: float = 1.4
@export var buff_color: Color = Color(
	1.0, 0.8, 0.8, 1.0
)

var _parent: Node2D
var _check_timer: float = 0.0
var _current_ally_count: int = 0
var _current_multiplier: float = 1.0
var _base_scale: Vector2 = Vector2.ONE


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"PackBuff parent must be Node2D"
	)
	_base_scale = _parent.scale


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	_check_timer += delta
	if _check_timer < CHECK_INTERVAL:
		return
	_check_timer = 0.0
	_update_buff()


func get_speed_multiplier() -> float:
	return _current_multiplier


func get_ally_count() -> int:
	return _current_ally_count


func _update_buff() -> void:
	var count: int = _count_nearby_allies()
	if count == _current_ally_count:
		return

	_current_ally_count = count
	_current_multiplier = _calc_multiplier(
		count
	)
	_apply_visuals(count)
	buff_changed.emit(
		count, _current_multiplier
	)


func _count_nearby_allies() -> int:
	var allies: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			ally_group
		)
	)
	var count: int = 0
	for node: Node in allies:
		if node == _parent:
			continue
		var n2d: Node2D = node as Node2D
		if not n2d or not is_instance_valid(n2d):
			continue
		var dist: float = (
			_parent.global_position.distance_to(
				n2d.global_position
			)
		)
		if dist <= detection_range:
			count += 1
	return count


func _calc_multiplier(count: int) -> float:
	return minf(
		1.0 + count * speed_bonus_per_ally,
		max_speed_multiplier,
	)


func _apply_visuals(count: int) -> void:
	if count > 0:
		var s: float = minf(
			1.0 + count * scale_per_ally,
			max_scale,
		)
		_parent.scale = _base_scale * s
		_parent.modulate = buff_color
	else:
		_parent.scale = _base_scale
		_parent.modulate = Color.WHITE

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/ecosystem/predator_behavior.gd ---
class_name PredatorBehavior
extends Node

"""Hunts nearby entities and eats them on contact.

Searches for targets in a configurable group,
moves toward the closest one, and calls die()
on contact. After eating, enters a cooldown
before hunting again.

Requires the parent to have an AnimatedSprite2D
for flip. Targets must have a die() method
(i.e. use the Npc orchestrator).
"""

signal target_acquired(target: Node2D)
signal target_eaten(target: Node2D)
signal hunt_started()
signal hunt_ended()

const MIN_EAT_DISTANCE: float = 12.0

@export var prey_group: String = "prey"
@export var speed: float = 70.0
@export var detection_range: float = 200.0
@export var eat_cooldown: float = 3.0
@export var flip_sprite: bool = true
@export var eat_animation: String = ""

var _parent: Node2D
var _target: Node2D = null
var _hunting: bool = false
var _paused: bool = false
var _cooldown_remaining: float = 0.0


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"PredatorBehavior parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return

	if _cooldown_remaining > 0.0:
		_cooldown_remaining -= delta
		return

	_find_target()

	if not _target:
		_set_hunting(false)
		return

	var dist: float = (
		_parent.global_position.distance_to(
			_target.global_position
		)
	)

	if dist < MIN_EAT_DISTANCE:
		_eat_target()
		return

	_set_hunting(true)
	var dir: Vector2 = (
		_target.global_position
		- _parent.global_position
	).normalized()
	_parent.position += dir * speed * delta

	if flip_sprite:
		_apply_flip(dir.x)


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true
	_set_hunting(false)


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func is_hunting() -> bool:
	return _hunting


func _find_target() -> void:
	if _valid_target(_target):
		var dist: float = (
			_parent.global_position.distance_to(
				_target.global_position
			)
		)
		if dist <= detection_range:
			return

	_target = null
	var best_dist: float = detection_range
	var candidates: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			prey_group
		)
	)

	for node: Node in candidates:
		if node == _parent:
			continue
		var n2d: Node2D = node as Node2D
		if not n2d:
			continue
		var d: float = (
			_parent.global_position.distance_to(
				n2d.global_position
			)
		)
		if d < best_dist:
			best_dist = d
			_target = n2d

	if _target:
		target_acquired.emit(_target)


func _eat_target() -> void:
	var eaten: Node2D = _target
	_target = null
	_cooldown_remaining = eat_cooldown
	_set_hunting(false)

	_play_eat_animation()
	target_eaten.emit(eaten)

	if eaten.has_method("die"):
		eaten.die()
	else:
		eaten.queue_free()


func _play_eat_animation() -> void:
	if eat_animation == "":
		return
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if not sprite:
		return
	if sprite.sprite_frames.has_animation(
		eat_animation
	):
		sprite.play(eat_animation)


func _set_hunting(value: bool) -> void:
	if value == _hunting:
		return
	_hunting = value
	if _hunting:
		hunt_started.emit()
	else:
		hunt_ended.emit()


func _valid_target(t: Node2D) -> bool:
	return t and is_instance_valid(t)


func _apply_flip(dir_x: float) -> void:
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if sprite and abs(dir_x) > 0.01:
		sprite.flip_h = dir_x < 0.0

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/ecosystem/split_on_death.gd ---
class_name SplitOnDeath
extends Node

"""Spawns smaller entities when the parent dies.

Connect to the parent Npc.died signal. On death,
instantiates split_scene N times around the death
position with a burst scatter effect.

The split children can themselves have SplitOnDeath
for recursive splitting (slime → mini-slime →
micro-slime).
"""

signal split_complete(children: Array[Node2D])

const SCATTER_SPEED: float = 120.0
const SCATTER_DURATION: float = 0.3

@export var split_scene: PackedScene
@export var split_count: int = 2
@export var child_scale: float = 0.6
@export var add_to_group: String = ""

var _parent: Node2D


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"SplitOnDeath parent must be Node2D"
	)
	if _parent.has_signal("died"):
		_parent.died.connect(_on_parent_died)


func _on_parent_died() -> void:
	if not split_scene:
		return

	var origin: Vector2 = (
		_parent.global_position
	)
	var scene_root: Node = (
		_parent.get_tree().current_scene
	)
	var children: Array[Node2D] = []
	var angle_step: float = (
		TAU / float(split_count)
	)

	for i: int in split_count:
		var entity: Node2D = (
			split_scene.instantiate() as Node2D
		)
		if not entity:
			continue

		scene_root.call_deferred(
			"add_child", entity
		)
		entity.global_position = origin
		entity.scale = Vector2.ONE * child_scale

		if add_to_group != "":
			entity.add_to_group(add_to_group)

		var angle: float = angle_step * i
		var dir: Vector2 = Vector2(
			cos(angle), sin(angle)
		)
		_scatter(entity, dir)
		children.append(entity)

	split_complete.emit(children)


func _scatter(
	entity: Node2D, dir: Vector2,
) -> void:
	"""Launch the child outward briefly."""
	var target: Vector2 = (
		entity.global_position
		+ dir * SCATTER_SPEED * SCATTER_DURATION
	)
	var tween: Tween = entity.create_tween()
	tween.tween_property(
		entity,
		"global_position",
		target,
		SCATTER_DURATION,
	).set_ease(
		Tween.EASE_OUT
	).set_trans(Tween.TRANS_QUAD)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/interaction/choice_display.gd ---
class_name ChoiceDisplay
extends Control

"""Displays two choice labels during dialog branching.

Shows key bindings and choice text. Emits
choice_picked with the selected index (0 for A,
1 for B). Listens for interact / interact_alt
input while visible.
"""

const CHOICE_A_INDEX: int = 0
const CHOICE_B_INDEX: int = 1

signal choice_picked(index: int)

var _active: bool = false

@onready var _label_a: Label = $VBox/LabelA
@onready var _label_b: Label = $VBox/LabelB


func _ready() -> void:
	visible = false
	input_helper.device_changed.connect(
		_on_device_changed
	)


func show_choices(
	text_a: String, text_b: String
) -> void:
	"""Display two choices and wait for input."""
	_update_labels(text_a, text_b)
	visible = true
	_active = true


func dismiss() -> void:
	visible = false
	_active = false


func _input(event: InputEvent) -> void:
	if not _active:
		return
	if event.is_action_pressed("interact"):
		_active = false
		visible = false
		choice_picked.emit(CHOICE_A_INDEX)
	elif event.is_action_pressed("interact_alt"):
		_active = false
		visible = false
		choice_picked.emit(CHOICE_B_INDEX)


func _update_labels(
	text_a: String, text_b: String
) -> void:
	var key_a: String = (
		input_helper.get_action_label("interact")
	)
	var key_b: String = (
		input_helper.get_action_label("interact_alt")
	)
	_label_a.text = "[%s] %s" % [key_a, text_a]
	_label_b.text = "[%s] %s" % [key_b, text_b]


func _on_device_changed(
	_is_joypad: bool
) -> void:
	if _active and _label_a and _label_b:
		_update_labels(
			_extract_text(_label_a.text),
			_extract_text(_label_b.text)
		)


func _extract_text(label_text: String) -> String:
	"""Strip the key prefix '[X] ' from a label."""
	var idx: int = label_text.find("] ")
	if idx == -1:
		return label_text
	return label_text.substr(idx + 2)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/interaction/collectible.gd ---
class_name Collectible
extends Node

"""Pickup behavior for items the player collects
on contact.

Detects player entering the parent's Area2D,
notifies a game manager, plays a pickup animation,
then removes the entity. Supports an initial
fall delay (coins that drop from above).

The parent must have an Area2D child for detection.
Drag it into the area export.
"""

signal collected(body: Node2D)

@export var area: Area2D
@export var animation_player: AnimationPlayer
@export var pickup_animation: String = "pickup"
@export var player_group: String = "player"
@export var game_manager_path: NodePath = ""
@export var fall_delay: float = 0.0
@export var fall_gravity: float = 98.0

var _parent: Node2D
var _game_manager: Node
var _falling: bool = false
var _velocity: Vector2 = Vector2.ZERO
var _grounded: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"Collectible parent must be Node2D"
	)

	if game_manager_path != NodePath(""):
		_game_manager = _parent.get_node_or_null(
			game_manager_path
		)

	if area:
		area.body_entered.connect(
			_on_body_entered
		)
		area.body_exited.connect(
			_on_body_exited
		)

	if fall_delay > 0.0:
		_start_fall_timer()


func _physics_process(delta: float) -> void:
	if not _falling:
		return
	if _grounded:
		return

	_velocity.y += fall_gravity * delta
	_parent.position += _velocity * delta


func _on_body_entered(body: Node2D) -> void:
	if body.is_in_group(player_group):
		_collect(body)
	else:
		_grounded = true
		_velocity = Vector2.ZERO


func _on_body_exited(_body: Node2D) -> void:
	_grounded = false


func _collect(body: Node2D) -> void:
	if area:
		var shape: CollisionShape2D = (
			area.get_node_or_null(
				"CollisionShape2D"
			)
		)
		if shape:
			shape.queue_free()

	if (
		_game_manager
		and _game_manager.has_method(
			"refresh_collected"
		)
	):
		_game_manager.refresh_collected(1)

	collected.emit(body)

	if (
		animation_player
		and animation_player.has_animation(
			pickup_animation
		)
	):
		animation_player.play(pickup_animation)
		await animation_player.animation_finished

	_parent.queue_free()


func _start_fall_timer() -> void:
	_parent.set_physics_process(false)
	var timer := Timer.new()
	timer.wait_time = fall_delay
	timer.one_shot = true
	_parent.add_child(timer)
	timer.timeout.connect(_on_fall_timer)
	timer.start()


func _on_fall_timer() -> void:
	_falling = true
	_parent.set_physics_process(true)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/interaction/dialog_controller.gd ---
class_name DialogController
extends Node

"""Manages dialog selection, page display, and
optional A/B choice branching.

Drives a TypewriterDisplay bubble through pages.
When the current dialog has choices, presents them
via an optional ChoiceDisplay, then either ends
(choice A) or plays alternate pages (choice B).

Drag Bubble and ChoiceDisplay into their export
slots in the editor.
"""

enum State {
	IDLE,
	PLAYING_PAGES,
	WAITING_CHOICE,
	PLAYING_CHOICE_B,
}

signal dialog_started(dialog: NpcDialog)
signal dialog_ended(
	dialog: NpcDialog,
	rewards: Array[DialogReward],
)
signal choices_presented(dialog: NpcDialog)

@export var dialogs: Array[NpcDialog] = []
@export var bubble: TypewriterDisplay
@export var choice_display: ChoiceDisplay

var _state: State = State.IDLE
var _current_dialog: NpcDialog = null
var _used_dialog_ids: Array[String] = []


func _ready() -> void:
	if bubble:
		bubble.all_pages_finished.connect(
			_on_all_pages_finished
		)
	if choice_display:
		choice_display.choice_picked.connect(
			_on_choice_picked
		)


func is_active() -> bool:
	return _state != State.IDLE


func is_waiting_choice() -> bool:
	return _state == State.WAITING_CHOICE


func start() -> void:
	if _state != State.IDLE:
		return

	_current_dialog = _select_dialog()
	if not _current_dialog:
		return

	_state = State.PLAYING_PAGES
	dialog_started.emit(_current_dialog)
	bubble.show_pages(_current_dialog.pages, true)


func advance() -> void:
	"""Advance pages. Ignored during choice wait."""
	if _state == State.WAITING_CHOICE:
		return
	if _state in [
		State.PLAYING_PAGES,
		State.PLAYING_CHOICE_B,
	]:
		bubble.try_advance()


func dismiss() -> void:
	"""Force-end everything (player walked away)."""
	if _state == State.IDLE:
		return
	if choice_display:
		choice_display.dismiss()
	_finish(_current_dialog.rewards)


func _on_all_pages_finished() -> void:
	if _state == State.PLAYING_PAGES:
		_on_main_pages_done()
	elif _state == State.PLAYING_CHOICE_B:
		_finish(_current_dialog.choice_b_rewards)


func _on_main_pages_done() -> void:
	var has: bool = (
		_current_dialog
		and _current_dialog.has_choices()
		and choice_display != null
	)
	if not has:
		_finish(_current_dialog.rewards)
		return

	_state = State.WAITING_CHOICE
	choices_presented.emit(_current_dialog)
	choice_display.show_choices(
		_current_dialog.choice_a_label,
		_current_dialog.choice_b_label,
	)


func _on_choice_picked(index: int) -> void:
	if _state != State.WAITING_CHOICE:
		return

	if index == ChoiceDisplay.CHOICE_A_INDEX:
		_finish(_current_dialog.rewards)
		return

	if _current_dialog.choice_b_pages.is_empty():
		_finish(_current_dialog.choice_b_rewards)
		return

	_state = State.PLAYING_CHOICE_B
	bubble.show_pages(
		_current_dialog.choice_b_pages, true
	)


func _finish(
	given_rewards: Array[DialogReward],
) -> void:
	if _state == State.IDLE:
		return

	bubble.dismiss()
	var finished: NpcDialog = _current_dialog

	if finished and finished.one_shot:
		if finished.dialog_id != "":
			_used_dialog_ids.append(
				finished.dialog_id
			)

	_state = State.IDLE
	_current_dialog = null
	dialog_ended.emit(finished, given_rewards)


func _select_dialog() -> NpcDialog:
	"""Pick the highest-priority valid dialog.

	Returns:
		The best matching NpcDialog, or null.
	"""
	var candidates: Array[NpcDialog] = []

	for d: NpcDialog in dialogs:
		if _is_filtered_out(d):
			continue
		candidates.append(d)

	if candidates.is_empty():
		return null

	candidates.sort_custom(
		func(
			a: NpcDialog, b: NpcDialog
		) -> bool:
			return a.priority > b.priority
	)
	return candidates[0]


func _is_filtered_out(d: NpcDialog) -> bool:
	if d.one_shot and d.dialog_id in _used_dialog_ids:
		return true
	if d.required_item == "":
		return false
	return not inventory.has_item(
		d.required_item, d.required_quantity
	)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/interaction/interaction_detector.gd ---
class_name InteractionDetector
extends Area2D

"""Detects player proximity and forwards interaction
input as signals.

Emits interacted() for the primary action and
interacted_alt() for the secondary action.
Add a CollisionShape2D as child.

Requires input actions: 'interact', 'interact_alt'.
"""

signal player_entered()
signal player_exited()
signal interacted()
signal interacted_alt()

var _player_in_range: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	body_entered.connect(_on_body_entered)
	body_exited.connect(_on_body_exited)


func _input(event: InputEvent) -> void:
	if not _player_in_range:
		return
	if event.is_action_pressed("interact"):
		interacted.emit()
	elif event.is_action_pressed("interact_alt"):
		interacted_alt.emit()


func is_player_in_range() -> bool:
	return _player_in_range


func _on_body_entered(body: Node2D) -> void:
	if body.is_in_group("player"):
		_player_in_range = true
		player_entered.emit()


func _on_body_exited(body: Node2D) -> void:
	if body.is_in_group("player"):
		_player_in_range = false
		player_exited.emit()

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/interaction/power_up.gd ---
class_name PowerUp
extends Node

"""Applies an effect to the player on contact,
then destroys the entity.

Configurable via exports: which property to modify,
the new value, and an optional duration after which
the original value is restored.

Plays a sound, spawns an explosion, runs a
disappear animation, then removes the entity.
"""

signal activated(body: Node2D)

@export var area: Area2D
@export var animation_player: AnimationPlayer
@export var audio_player: AudioStreamPlayer2D
@export var explosion_scene: PackedScene
@export var sounds: Array[AudioStreamPlayer2D] = []

@export_group("Effect")
@export var player_property: String = (
	"max_horizontal_speed"
)
@export var property_value: float = 600.0
@export var effect_duration: float = 0.0
@export var disappear_animation: String = (
	"disappear"
)
@export var player_group: String = "player"

var _parent: Node2D


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"PowerUp parent must be Node2D"
	)
	if area:
		area.body_entered.connect(
			_on_body_entered
		)


func _on_body_entered(body: Node2D) -> void:
	if not body.is_in_group(player_group):
		return
	_apply_effect(body)
	activated.emit(body)
	_play_feedback()


func _apply_effect(body: Node2D) -> void:
	if player_property == "":
		return
	if not body.get(player_property) == null:
		var old_value: float = body.get(
			player_property
		)
		body.set(player_property, property_value)

		if effect_duration > 0.0:
			_schedule_restore(
				body, old_value
			)
	else:
		body.set(player_property, property_value)


func _schedule_restore(
	body: Node2D, old_value: float,
) -> void:
	var tree: SceneTree = _parent.get_tree()
	var timer: SceneTreeTimer = (
		tree.create_timer(effect_duration)
	)
	timer.timeout.connect(
		func() -> void:
			if is_instance_valid(body):
				body.set(
					player_property,
					old_value,
				)
	)


func _play_feedback() -> void:
	if area:
		area.queue_free()

	_spawn_explosion()
	_play_sound()
	_play_disappear()


func _spawn_explosion() -> void:
	if not explosion_scene:
		return
	var fx: Node = explosion_scene.instantiate()
	fx.position = _parent.global_position
	fx.rotation = _parent.global_rotation
	if fx is GPUParticles2D:
		fx.emitting = true
	_parent.get_tree().current_scene.add_child(
		fx
	)


func _play_sound() -> void:
	if sounds.is_empty() or not audio_player:
		return
	global.play_rand_sound(
		audio_player, sounds
	)


func _play_disappear() -> void:
	if not animation_player:
		_parent.queue_free()
		return
	if not animation_player.has_animation(
		disappear_animation
	):
		_parent.queue_free()
		return

	animation_player.play(disappear_animation)
	animation_player.animation_finished.connect(
		func(_anim: StringName) -> void:
			_parent.queue_free()
	)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/interaction/prompt_display.gd ---
class_name PromptDisplay
extends Label

"""Shows an interaction prompt adapting to the current
input device. Displays both interact and interact_alt
key labels when the entity supports choices."""

@export var action_name: String = "interact"
@export var action_alt_name: String = "interact_alt"
@export var prompt_key: String = "PROMPT_INTERACT"
@export var show_alt_hint: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	visible = false
	_update_text()
	input_helper.device_changed.connect(
		_on_device_changed
	)


func show_prompt() -> void:
	visible = true


func hide_prompt() -> void:
	visible = false


func _update_text() -> void:
	var key_a: String = (
		input_helper.get_action_label(action_name)
	)
	if show_alt_hint:
		var key_b: String = (
			input_helper.get_action_label(
				action_alt_name
			)
		)
		text = "[%s] Talk  [%s] Alt" % [key_a, key_b]
	else:
		text = tr(prompt_key) % key_a


func _on_device_changed(_is_joypad: bool) -> void:
	_update_text()

class_name StateDoor
extends Node

"""Two-state door that transitions the player to
the next level.

Starts locked. Call open() to unlock. When the
player enters the open door's Area2D, triggers
level transition via global.go_to_next_level().

Also listens to the 'next_level' input action as
a debug shortcut.
"""

enum State { LOCKED, OPEN }

signal door_opened()
signal player_entered_door(body: Node2D)

@export var area: Area2D
@export var animation_player: AnimationPlayer
@export var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D
@export var particles: GPUParticles2D
@export var open_animation: String = "open_door"
@export var locked_frame: String = "locked"
@export var open_frame: String = "open"

var _state: State = State.LOCKED


func _ready() -> void:
	if area:
		area.body_entered.connect(
			_on_body_entered
		)


func _input(event: InputEvent) -> void:
	if event.is_action_pressed("next_level"):
		global.go_to_next_level(null, null)


func open() -> void:
	"""Unlock the door with particles and
	animation."""
	if _state == State.OPEN:
		return
	_state = State.OPEN

	if particles and not particles.emitting:
		particles.emitting = true
	if animation_player:
		animation_player.play(open_animation)

	door_opened.emit()


func is_open() -> bool:
	return _state == State.OPEN


func _on_body_entered(body: Node2D) -> void:
	if not body is PlayerController:
		return
	if _state != State.OPEN:
		return
	if (
		sprite
		and sprite.animation != open_frame
	):
		return

	player_entered_door.emit(body)
	global.go_to_next_level(body, get_parent())

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/loot/item_dropper.gd ---
class_name ItemDropper
extends Node2D

"""Spawns collectible items when triggered.

Call drop() to scatter items around the parent
position. Each drop entry defines an item scene,
quantity, and drop chance.

Works for both monsters (drop on death) and NPCs
(drop on dialog end, quest completion, etc.).
"""

const SCATTER_RADIUS: float = 20.0
const LAUNCH_HEIGHT: float = -60.0
const LAUNCH_DURATION: float = 0.5
const BOUNCE_HEIGHT: float = -15.0
const BOUNCE_DURATION: float = 0.25

signal items_dropped(count: int)

@export var drop_table: Array[DropEntry] = []


func drop() -> void:
	"""Scatter all valid drops from the table."""
	var parent: Node2D = get_parent() as Node2D
	if not parent:
		return

	var origin: Vector2 = parent.global_position
	var scene_root: Node = (
		parent.get_tree().current_scene
	)
	var count: int = 0

	for entry: DropEntry in drop_table:
		if not entry.item_scene:
			continue
		for i: int in entry.quantity:
			if not _roll(entry.drop_chance):
				continue
			var item: Node2D = (
				entry.item_scene.instantiate()
			)
			scene_root.add_child(item)
			item.global_position = origin
			_animate_scatter(item, origin)
			count += 1

	if count > 0:
		items_dropped.emit(count)


func _roll(chance: float) -> bool:
	return randf() <= chance


func _animate_scatter(
	item: Node2D, origin: Vector2,
) -> void:
	"""Launch item up then let it fall with a bounce.
	"""
	var offset_x: float = randf_range(
		-SCATTER_RADIUS, SCATTER_RADIUS
	)
	var land: Vector2 = Vector2(
		origin.x + offset_x, origin.y
	)

	var tween: Tween = item.create_tween()
	tween.set_parallel(false)

	tween.tween_property(
		item,
		"global_position",
		Vector2(land.x, origin.y + LAUNCH_HEIGHT),
		LAUNCH_DURATION * 0.5,
	).set_ease(
		Tween.EASE_OUT
	).set_trans(Tween.TRANS_QUAD)

	tween.tween_property(
		item,
		"global_position",
		land,
		LAUNCH_DURATION * 0.5,
	).set_ease(
		Tween.EASE_IN
	).set_trans(Tween.TRANS_QUAD)

	tween.tween_property(
		item,
		"global_position:y",
		land.y + BOUNCE_HEIGHT,
		BOUNCE_DURATION * 0.5,
	).set_ease(
		Tween.EASE_OUT
	).set_trans(Tween.TRANS_QUAD)

	tween.tween_property(
		item,
		"global_position:y",
		land.y,
		BOUNCE_DURATION * 0.5,
	).set_ease(
		Tween.EASE_IN
	).set_trans(Tween.TRANS_QUAD)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/loot/reward_animator.gd ---
class_name RewardAnimator
extends Node2D

"""Plays a visual reward animation: floating item
labels rising up with a particle burst.

Attach as child of the NPC. Connect
RewardGiver.rewards_given to play().
Optionally assign an explosion PackedScene
(e.g. explosion.tscn) for the firework effect.
"""

const FLOAT_DISTANCE: float = 40.0
const FLOAT_DURATION: float = 1.2
const FADE_DELAY: float = 0.6
const FADE_DURATION: float = 0.6
const LINE_SPACING: float = 16.0
const FONT_SIZE: int = 8

@export var explosion_scene: PackedScene
@export var particle_color: Color = Color.GOLD
@export var label_color: Color = Color.YELLOW
@export var shadow_color: Color = Color.BLACK


func play(
	rewards: Array[DialogReward],
) -> void:
	"""Animate all rewards with labels + particles.

	Args:
		rewards: The rewards to display.
	"""
	_spawn_firework()

	var offset_y: float = 0.0
	for r: DialogReward in rewards:
		if r.item_id == "":
			continue
		_spawn_floating_label(r, offset_y)
		offset_y -= LINE_SPACING


func _spawn_firework() -> void:
	if explosion_scene:
		var fx: Node = explosion_scene.instantiate()
		add_child(fx)
		if fx is GPUParticles2D:
			fx.emitting = true
		return

	var particles := _build_particles()
	add_child(particles)
	particles.emitting = true

	var timer := get_tree().create_timer(
		particles.lifetime + 0.5
	)
	timer.timeout.connect(particles.queue_free)


func _spawn_floating_label(
	reward: DialogReward, y_offset: float
) -> void:
	var text: String = _format_reward(reward)
	var label := Label.new()
	label.text = text
	label.horizontal_alignment = (
		HORIZONTAL_ALIGNMENT_CENTER
	)
	label.add_theme_font_size_override(
		"font_size", FONT_SIZE
	)
	label.add_theme_color_override(
		"font_color", label_color
	)
	label.add_theme_color_override(
		"font_shadow_color", shadow_color
	)
	label.add_theme_constant_override(
		"shadow_offset_x", 1
	)
	label.add_theme_constant_override(
		"shadow_offset_y", 1
	)
	label.position = Vector2(-40, -20 + y_offset)
	label.size = Vector2(80, 20)
	add_child(label)

	var tween: Tween = create_tween()
	tween.set_parallel(true)
	tween.tween_property(
		label,
		"position:y",
		label.position.y - FLOAT_DISTANCE,
		FLOAT_DURATION,
	).set_ease(Tween.EASE_OUT).set_trans(
		Tween.TRANS_CUBIC
	)
	tween.tween_property(
		label,
		"modulate:a",
		0.0,
		FADE_DURATION,
	).set_delay(FADE_DELAY)
	tween.chain().tween_callback(label.queue_free)


func _build_particles() -> GPUParticles2D:
	"""Create a simple burst particle emitter."""
	var p := GPUParticles2D.new()
	p.amount = 24
	p.one_shot = true
	p.explosiveness = 1.0
	p.lifetime = 0.8

	var mat := ParticleProcessMaterial.new()
	mat.particle_flag_disable_z = true
	mat.spread = 180.0
	mat.initial_velocity_min = 60.0
	mat.initial_velocity_max = 120.0
	mat.gravity = Vector3(0, 40, 0)
	mat.scale_min = 2.0
	mat.scale_max = 4.0
	mat.color = particle_color
	p.process_material = mat

	return p


func _format_reward(r: DialogReward) -> String:
	if r.quantity > 1:
		return "+ %s x%d" % [r.item_id, r.quantity]
	return "+ %s" % r.item_id

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/loot/reward_giver.gd ---
class_name RewardGiver
extends Node

"""Distributes item rewards to the player inventory.

Emits rewards_given after all items are added.
Connect a RewardAnimator to rewards_given for
visual feedback.
"""

signal rewards_given(
	rewards: Array[DialogReward],
)


func give(
	dialog_rewards: Array[DialogReward],
) -> void:
	"""Add all rewards to the inventory.

	Args:
		dialog_rewards: Rewards to distribute.
	"""
	if dialog_rewards.is_empty():
		return

	for r: DialogReward in dialog_rewards:
		if r.item_id == "":
			continue
		inventory.add_item(r.item_id, r.quantity)

	rewards_given.emit(dialog_rewards)

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/movement/chase_movement.gd ---
class_name ChaseMovement
extends Node

"""Moves the parent Node2D toward the player.

Finds the player via the 'player' group.
Only chases when the player is within detection
range. Flips the sprite to face movement direction.
"""

signal started_chasing()
signal stopped_chasing()

const GROUP_PLAYER: String = "player"

@export var speed: float = 60.0
@export var detection_range: float = 150.0
@export var stop_distance: float = 10.0
@export var flip_sprite: bool = true

var _parent: Node2D
var _player: Node2D
var _chasing: bool = false
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"ChaseMovement parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		_set_chasing(false)
		return

	var dist: float = (
		_parent.global_position.distance_to(
			_player.global_position
		)
	)

	if dist > detection_range:
		_set_chasing(false)
		return

	if dist < stop_distance:
		_set_chasing(true)
		return

	_set_chasing(true)
	var dir: Vector2 = (
		_player.global_position
		- _parent.global_position
	).normalized()
	_parent.position += dir * speed * delta

	if flip_sprite:
		_apply_flip(dir.x)


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true
	_set_chasing(false)


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func is_chasing() -> bool:
	return _chasing


func _set_chasing(value: bool) -> void:
	if value == _chasing:
		return
	_chasing = value
	if _chasing:
		started_chasing.emit()
	else:
		stopped_chasing.emit()


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			GROUP_PLAYER
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D


func _apply_flip(dir_x: float) -> void:
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if sprite and abs(dir_x) > 0.01:
		sprite.flip_h = dir_x < 0.0

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/movement/flee_movement.gd ---
class_name FleeMovement
extends Node

"""Moves the parent Node2D away from the player.

Finds the player via the 'player' group.
Only flees when the player is within panic range.
Stops fleeing once the player is beyond safe range.
"""

signal started_fleeing()
signal stopped_fleeing()

const GROUP_PLAYER: String = "player"

@export var speed: float = 80.0
@export var panic_range: float = 100.0
@export var safe_range: float = 180.0
@export var flip_sprite: bool = true

var _parent: Node2D
var _player: Node2D
var _fleeing: bool = false
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"FleeMovement parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		_set_fleeing(false)
		return

	var dist: float = (
		_parent.global_position.distance_to(
			_player.global_position
		)
	)

	if not _fleeing and dist > panic_range:
		return
	if _fleeing and dist > safe_range:
		_set_fleeing(false)
		return

	_set_fleeing(true)
	var dir: Vector2 = (
		_parent.global_position
		- _player.global_position
	).normalized()
	_parent.position += dir * speed * delta

	if flip_sprite:
		_apply_flip(dir.x)


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true
	_set_fleeing(false)


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func is_fleeing() -> bool:
	return _fleeing


func _set_fleeing(value: bool) -> void:
	if value == _fleeing:
		return
	_fleeing = value
	if _fleeing:
		started_fleeing.emit()
	else:
		stopped_fleeing.emit()


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			GROUP_PLAYER
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D


func _apply_flip(dir_x: float) -> void:
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if sprite and abs(dir_x) > 0.01:
		sprite.flip_h = dir_x < 0.0

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/movement/follow_ally.gd ---
class_name FollowAlly
extends Node

"""Follows the player as a friendly companion for a
limited duration.

Starts inactive. Call activate() to begin following.
After follow_duration seconds, emits follow_ended
and stops. Can be reactivated.

Unlike ChaseMovement this is a friendly behavior:
no kill intent, smoother trailing distance, and an
optional happy animation while following.
"""

signal follow_started()
signal follow_ended()

const GROUP_PLAYER: String = "player"

@export var speed: float = 100.0
@export var follow_distance: float = 25.0
@export var follow_duration: float = 15.0
@export var follow_animation: String = ""
@export var flip_sprite: bool = true

var _parent: Node2D
var _player: Node2D
var _active: bool = false
var _paused: bool = false
var _remaining: float = 0.0


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"FollowAlly parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if not _active or _paused:
		return

	_remaining -= delta
	if _remaining <= 0.0:
		deactivate()
		return

	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		return

	var dist: float = (
		_parent.global_position.distance_to(
			_player.global_position
		)
	)
	if dist <= follow_distance:
		return

	var dir: Vector2 = (
		_player.global_position
		- _parent.global_position
	).normalized()
	_parent.position += dir * speed * delta

	if flip_sprite:
		_apply_flip(dir.x)


func activate(
	duration: float = -1.0,
) -> void:
	"""Start following the player.

	Args:
		duration: Override follow time, or -1 to
			use the export default.
	"""
	if duration > 0.0:
		_remaining = duration
	else:
		_remaining = follow_duration
	_active = true
	_play_follow_anim()
	follow_started.emit()


func deactivate() -> void:
	_active = false
	_remaining = 0.0
	follow_ended.emit()


func pause() -> void:
	"""Temporarily stop following without resetting
	the remaining timer."""
	_paused = true


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func is_active() -> bool:
	return _active


func get_remaining_time() -> float:
	return _remaining


func _play_follow_anim() -> void:
	if follow_animation == "":
		return
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if not sprite or not sprite.sprite_frames:
		return
	if sprite.sprite_frames.has_animation(
		follow_animation
	):
		sprite.play(follow_animation)


func _apply_flip(dir_x: float) -> void:
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null(
			"AnimatedSprite2D"
		)
	)
	if sprite and abs(dir_x) > 0.01:
		sprite.flip_h = dir_x < 0.0


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			GROUP_PLAYER
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/movement/patrol_movement.gd ---
class_name PatrolMovement
extends Node

"""Moves the parent Node2D horizontally, reversing
direction when raycasts detect walls or edges.

Add two RayCast2D children named RayCastRight and
RayCastLeft to the parent, or assign them via
exports.
"""

signal direction_changed(new_direction: int)

@export var speed: float = 40.0
@export var ray_right: RayCast2D
@export var ray_left: RayCast2D
@export var flip_sprite: bool = true

var _direction: int = 1
var _paused: bool = false
var _parent: Node2D


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"PatrolMovement parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return
	_check_raycasts()
	_parent.position.x += (
		_direction * speed * delta
	)
	if flip_sprite:
		_apply_flip()


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func get_direction() -> int:
	return _direction


func _check_raycasts() -> void:
	if ray_right and ray_right.is_colliding():
		_set_direction(-1)
	elif ray_left and ray_left.is_colliding():
		_set_direction(1)


func _set_direction(d: int) -> void:
	if d == _direction:
		return
	_direction = d
	direction_changed.emit(_direction)


func _apply_flip() -> void:
	var sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
		_parent.get_node_or_null("AnimatedSprite2D")
	)
	if sprite:
		sprite.flip_h = _direction < 0

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/movement/rotate_toward_player.gd ---
class_name RotateTowardPlayer
extends Node

"""Smoothly rotates the parent Node2D to face the
player.

Finds the player via the 'player' group.
Replaces the old clock.gd behavior as a composable
component.
"""

const GROUP_PLAYER: String = "player"
const ANGLE_OFFSET: float = PI / 2.0

@export var rotation_speed: float = 1.0
@export var target_offset: Vector2 = Vector2(0, -12)

var _parent: Node2D
var _player: Node2D
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"RotateTowardPlayer parent must be Node2D"
	)


func _process(delta: float) -> void:
	if _paused:
		return
	_find_player()
	if not _player:
		return

	var target_pos: Vector2 = (
		_player.global_position + target_offset
	)
	var direction: Vector2 = (
		target_pos - _parent.global_position
	)
	var target_angle: float = (
		direction.angle() + ANGLE_OFFSET
	)
	_parent.rotation = lerp_angle(
		_parent.rotation,
		target_angle,
		rotation_speed * delta,
	)


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false


func _find_player() -> void:
	if _player and is_instance_valid(_player):
		return
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			GROUP_PLAYER
		)
	)
	if not players.is_empty():
		_player = players[0] as Node2D

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/components/movement/teleport_movement.gd ---
class_name TeleportMovement
extends Node

"""Teleports the parent to random positions.

Blinks to a new spot within radius every N seconds.
Plays a fade-out / fade-in animation on each
teleport. Optionally avoids teleporting too close
to the player.
"""

signal teleported(new_position: Vector2)

const FADE_DURATION: float = 0.2

@export var teleport_interval: float = 3.0
@export var teleport_radius: float = 80.0
@export var min_player_distance: float = 30.0
@export var anchor_to_start: bool = true

var _parent: Node2D
var _origin: Vector2
var _timer: Timer
var _paused: bool = false


func _ready() -> void:
	_parent = get_parent() as Node2D
	assert(
		_parent != null,
		"TeleportMovement parent must be Node2D"
	)
	_origin = _parent.global_position

	_timer = Timer.new()
	_timer.wait_time = teleport_interval
	_timer.one_shot = false
	_timer.timeout.connect(_on_timer)
	add_child(_timer)
	_timer.start()


func pause() -> void:
	_paused = true
	_timer.stop()


func resume() -> void:
	_paused = false
	_timer.start()


func teleport_now() -> void:
	"""Force an immediate teleport."""
	_do_teleport()


func _on_timer() -> void:
	if _paused:
		return
	_do_teleport()


func _do_teleport() -> void:
	var target: Vector2 = _pick_position()
	_animate_blink(target)


func _pick_position() -> Vector2:
	var center: Vector2 = (
		_origin if anchor_to_start
		else _parent.global_position
	)
	var player_pos: Vector2 = _get_player_pos()

	for attempt: int in 10:
		var angle: float = randf() * TAU
		var dist: float = (
			randf() * teleport_radius
		)
		var candidate: Vector2 = center + Vector2(
			cos(angle) * dist,
			sin(angle) * dist,
		)
		if player_pos == Vector2.ZERO:
			return candidate
		var d: float = (
			candidate.distance_to(player_pos)
		)
		if d >= min_player_distance:
			return candidate

	return center


func _animate_blink(
	target: Vector2,
) -> void:
	var tween: Tween = _parent.create_tween()
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "modulate:a",
		0.0, FADE_DURATION,
	)
	tween.tween_callback(
		_move_to.bind(target)
	)
	tween.tween_property(
		_parent, "modulate:a",
		1.0, FADE_DURATION,
	)


func _move_to(pos: Vector2) -> void:
	_parent.global_position = pos
	teleported.emit(pos)


func _get_player_pos() -> Vector2:
	var players: Array[Node] = (
		_parent.get_tree().get_nodes_in_group(
			"player"
		)
	)
	if players.is_empty():
		return Vector2.ZERO
	var p: Node2D = players[0] as Node2D
	if p:
		return p.global_position
	return Vector2.ZERO

--- END OF FILE ---

class_name NpcDialog
extends Resource

"""Data container for a single NPC dialog sequence.

Supports optional branching via choices. When
choice_a_label is set, the dialog presents two
options after its pages finish:
- Choice A: ends dialog, gives rewards.
- Choice B: plays choice_b_pages, then gives
  choice_b_rewards.

When choice_a_label is empty, the dialog ends
normally after pages with rewards given
automatically (classic behavior).
"""

@export var dialog_id: String = ""
@export_multiline var pages: Array[String] = []

@export_group("Conditions")
@export var required_item: String = ""
@export var required_quantity: int = 1

@export_group("Rewards")
@export var rewards: Array[DialogReward] = []

@export_group("Choices")
@export var choice_a_label: String = ""
@export var choice_b_label: String = ""
@export_multiline var choice_b_pages: Array[String] = []
@export var choice_b_rewards: Array[DialogReward] = []

@export_group("Behavior")
@export var one_shot: bool = false
@export var priority: int = 0


func has_choices() -> bool:
	return choice_a_label != ""

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/entity.gd ---
class_name Entity
extends Node2D

"""Unified entity orchestrator.

Wires child components together via signals. Every
component export is optional: the entity's behavior
is defined entirely by which children are present.

Works for NPCs, monsters, coins, doors, power-ups,
or any game object that interacts with the world.
"""

signal died()

@export var entity_name: String = "Entity"
@export var idle_animation: String = "idle"

@export_group("Interaction")
@export var interaction_detector: InteractionDetector
@export var prompt_display: PromptDisplay
@export var dialog_controller: DialogController
@export var reward_giver: RewardGiver
@export var reward_animator: RewardAnimator
@export var collectible: Collectible
@export var power_up: PowerUp
@export var state_door: StateDoor

@export_group("Movement")
@export var patrol_movement: PatrolMovement
@export var chase_movement: ChaseMovement
@export var flee_movement: FleeMovement
@export var rotate_toward_player: RotateTowardPlayer
@export var teleport_movement: TeleportMovement
@export var follow_ally: FollowAlly

@export_group("Loot")
@export var item_dropper: ItemDropper

@export_group("Combat")
@export var dash_attack: DashAttack
@export var mimic_behavior: MimicBehavior
@export var burrow_behavior: BurrowBehavior

@export_group("Ecosystem")
@export var predator_behavior: PredatorBehavior
@export var entity_spawner: EntitySpawner
@export var mutation_behavior: MutationBehavior
@export var split_on_death: SplitOnDeath
@export var pack_buff: PackBuff

@onready var _sprite: AnimatedSprite2D = (
	get_node_or_null("AnimatedSprite2D")
)


func _ready() -> void:
	_play_idle()
	_wire_interaction()
	_wire_dialog()
	_wire_rewards()
	_wire_movement_pause()


# -------------------------------------------------
#  Death / Destruction
# -------------------------------------------------

func die() -> void:
	"""Kill this entity: drop items, then remove."""
	if item_dropper:
		item_dropper.drop()
	died.emit()
	queue_free()


# -------------------------------------------------
#  Idle animation
# -------------------------------------------------

func _play_idle() -> void:
	if not _sprite or not _sprite.sprite_frames:
		return
	if _sprite.sprite_frames.has_animation(
		idle_animation
	):
		_sprite.play(idle_animation)


# -------------------------------------------------
#  Wiring: InteractionDetector ↔ Prompt / Dialog
# -------------------------------------------------

func _wire_interaction() -> void:
	if not interaction_detector:
		return
	interaction_detector.player_entered.connect(
		_on_player_entered
	)
	interaction_detector.player_exited.connect(
		_on_player_exited
	)
	interaction_detector.interacted.connect(
		_on_interacted
	)


func _on_player_entered() -> void:
	if _dialog_active():
		return
	if prompt_display:
		prompt_display.show_prompt()


func _on_player_exited() -> void:
	if prompt_display:
		prompt_display.hide_prompt()
	if _dialog_active():
		dialog_controller.dismiss()


func _on_interacted() -> void:
	if not dialog_controller:
		return
	if _dialog_active():
		dialog_controller.advance()
		return
	_start_talking()


# -------------------------------------------------
#  Wiring: DialogController → Rewards
# -------------------------------------------------

func _wire_dialog() -> void:
	if not dialog_controller:
		return
	dialog_controller.dialog_started.connect(
		_on_dialog_started
	)
	dialog_controller.dialog_ended.connect(
		_on_dialog_ended
	)


func _on_dialog_started(
	_dialog: NpcDialog,
) -> void:
	if prompt_display:
		prompt_display.hide_prompt()


func _on_dialog_ended(
	_dialog: NpcDialog,
	rewards: Array[DialogReward],
) -> void:
	if reward_giver and not rewards.is_empty():
		reward_giver.give(rewards)
	if _player_here() and prompt_display:
		prompt_display.show_prompt()


# -------------------------------------------------
#  Wiring: RewardGiver → RewardAnimator
# -------------------------------------------------

func _wire_rewards() -> void:
	if not reward_giver or not reward_animator:
		return
	reward_giver.rewards_given.connect(
		reward_animator.play
	)


# -------------------------------------------------
#  Wiring: Pause all pausable components on dialog
# -------------------------------------------------

func _wire_movement_pause() -> void:
	if not dialog_controller:
		return

	var pausables: Array[Node] = (
		_collect_pausables()
	)
	for node: Node in pausables:
		dialog_controller.dialog_started.connect(
			_make_pause_cb(node)
		)
		dialog_controller.dialog_ended.connect(
			_make_resume_cb(node)
		)


func _collect_pausables() -> Array[Node]:
	var result: Array[Node] = []
	var candidates: Array[Node] = [
		patrol_movement,
		chase_movement,
		flee_movement,
		rotate_toward_player,
		teleport_movement,
		follow_ally,
		predator_behavior,
		entity_spawner,
		mutation_behavior,
		dash_attack,
		mimic_behavior,
		burrow_behavior,
	]
	for c: Node in candidates:
		if c and c.has_method("pause"):
			result.append(c)
	return result


func _make_pause_cb(
	node: Node,
) -> Callable:
	return func(_d: NpcDialog) -> void:
		node.pause()


func _make_resume_cb(
	node: Node,
) -> Callable:
	return func(
		_d: NpcDialog,
		_r: Array[DialogReward],
	) -> void:
		node.resume()


# -------------------------------------------------
#  Helpers
# -------------------------------------------------

func _start_talking() -> void:
	if prompt_display:
		prompt_display.hide_prompt()
	dialog_controller.start()


func _dialog_active() -> bool:
	return (
		dialog_controller
		and dialog_controller.is_active()
	)


func _player_here() -> bool:
	return (
		interaction_detector
		and interaction_detector.is_player_in_range()
	)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/entities_tmp/presets/dog.gd ---
class_name Dog
extends Entity

"""A dog that patrols, barks, and follows the player
after receiving a bone.

When the 'bone_gift' dialog ends, consumes the bone,
activates FollowAlly, and stops patrol. When the
follow timer expires, resumes patrol.
"""

const BONE_ITEM_ID: String = "bone"
const BONE_DIALOG_ID: String = "bone_gift"

@export_group("Dog")
@export var bark_animation: String = "bark"
@export var happy_animation: String = "happy"


func _ready() -> void:
	super._ready()
	_wire_dog()


func _wire_dog() -> void:
	if dialog_controller:
		dialog_controller.dialog_started.connect(
			_on_dog_dialog_started
		)
		dialog_controller.dialog_ended.connect(
			_on_dog_dialog_ended
		)
	if follow_ally:
		follow_ally.follow_started.connect(
			_on_follow_started
		)
		follow_ally.follow_ended.connect(
			_on_follow_ended
		)


func _on_dog_dialog_started(
	_dialog: NpcDialog,
) -> void:
	if patrol_movement:
		patrol_movement.pause()
	_play_anim(bark_animation)


func _on_dog_dialog_ended(
	dialog: NpcDialog,
	_rewards: Array[DialogReward],
) -> void:
	if not dialog:
		return

	if dialog.dialog_id == BONE_DIALOG_ID:
		_accept_bone()
		return

	if patrol_movement:
		patrol_movement.resume()
	_play_idle()


func _accept_bone() -> void:
	inventory.remove_item(BONE_ITEM_ID, 1)

	if follow_ally:
		if patrol_movement:
			patrol_movement.pause()
		_play_anim(happy_animation)
		follow_ally.activate()


func _on_follow_started() -> void:
	_play_anim(happy_animation)


func _on_follow_ended() -> void:
	if patrol_movement:
		patrol_movement.resume()
	_play_idle()


func _play_anim(anim_name: String) -> void:
	if not _sprite or not _sprite.sprite_frames:
		return
	if _sprite.sprite_frames.has_animation(
		anim_name
	):
		_sprite.play(anim_name)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/scripts/bottle.gd ---
extends Node2D

signal bottle_hit()

@export var sounds_hit: Array[AudioStreamMP3]
@export var explosion: PackedScene
@onready var area_2d = $Area2D
@onready var audio_stream_player = $AudioStreamPlayer
@onready var animation_player: AnimationPlayer = $AnimationPlayer

func _on_area_2d_body_entered(body):
	if body.is_in_group("player"):
		body.max_horizontal_speed = 600.0
		bottle_hit.emit()

func _on_bottle_hit():
	area_2d.queue_free()
	var p = explosion.instantiate()
	p.position = global_position
	p.rotation = global_rotation
	p.emitting = true
	get_tree().current_scene.add_child(p)
	global.play_rand_sound(audio_stream_player, sounds_hit)
	animation_player.play("disappear")
	await animation_player.animation_finished
	queue_free()

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/scripts/canvas_layer_for_all.gd ---
@tool
extends CanvasLayer

signal signal_btn_next_level()
signal signal_update_mobile_controls()

@export var label_for_level: String = "Level (to be filled)" : \
	set = _set_label_for_level, get = _get_label_for_level

@export var label_description_level: String = "Description (to be filled)" : \
	set = _set_label_description_level, get = _get_label_description_level

# To invert controls:
@export var mobile_left_right_positions: Array[Vector2]
@export var mobile_up_down_positions: Array[Vector2]

@onready var label_level = $LabelLevel
@onready var label_desc = $LabelDesc
@onready var mobile_left_right: Node2D = $mobile_left_right
@onready var mobile_up_down: Node2D = $mobile_up_down
@onready var options = $options
@onready var btn_next_level = $btn_next_level

func get_fade_in_out() -> Node2D:
	return find_child("fade_in_out", true, false)
	
func switch_mobile_controls():
	mobile_left_right.position = mobile_left_right_positions[1]
	mobile_left_right.switch_press_zones()
	mobile_up_down.position = mobile_up_down_positions[1]

func _ready():
	label_level.text = label_for_level
	label_desc.text = label_description_level
	if not Engine.is_editor_hint():
		emit_signal("signal_update_mobile_controls")

func _get_label_for_level() -> String:
	return label_for_level

func _set_label_for_level(new_value: String) -> void:
	label_for_level = new_value
	if label_level:
		label_level.text = new_value

func _get_label_description_level() -> String:
	return label_description_level

func _set_label_description_level(new_value: String) -> void:
	label_description_level = new_value
	if label_desc:
		label_desc.text = new_value

func _on_btn_next_level_pressed():
	btn_next_level.disabled = true
	emit_signal("signal_btn_next_level")

func _on_btn_options_pressed():
	#global.mobile_visible = not global.mobile_visible
	#mobile_left_right.visible = global.mobile_visible
	#mobile_up_down.visible = global.mobile_visible
	if Engine.is_editor_hint():  # in editor = do nothing:
		return
	options.visible = true


func _on_signal_update_mobile_controls():
	mobile_left_right.visible = global.show_mobile_controls
	mobile_up_down.visible = global.show_mobile_controls
	if global.are_mobile_controls_flipped:
		switch_mobile_controls()

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/scripts/clock.gd ---
extends Node2D

@export var player: NodePath 
@export var rotation_speed = 1.0

var _player_node: Node

func _ready():
	if not player:  # never call _process() again:
		set_physics_process(false)
	_player_node = get_node(player)
	if not _player_node:  # never call _process() again:
		set_physics_process(false)
	
func _process(delta):
	var player_position = _player_node.global_position
	player_position.y -= 12
	var direction = player_position - global_position
	var target_angle = direction.angle() + PI / 2
	rotation = lerp_angle(rotation, target_angle, rotation_speed * delta)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/scripts/coin.gd ---
extends Area2D

@onready var game_manager = $"../../GameManager"
@onready var animation_player = $AnimationPlayer
@export var delay_before_falling: float = 0.1
@export var falling_speed_gravity: int = 98
@onready var collision_shape_2d = $CollisionShape2D

@onready var timer = $Timer

var velocity: Vector2 = Vector2.ZERO
var is_touching: bool = false

func _ready():
	# (!) this will stop call _physics_process():
	set_physics_process(false)
	if delay_before_falling > 0:
		timer.start(delay_before_falling)
	
func _on_body_entered(body):
	if body.is_in_group("player"):
		collision_shape_2d.queue_free()
		game_manager.refresh_collected(1)
		animation_player.play("pickup")
	else:
		is_touching = true
		velocity = Vector2.ZERO
		falling_speed_gravity = 0

func _physics_process(delta):
	# Appliquer la gravité
	velocity.y += falling_speed_gravity  * delta
	
	# Déplacer l'Area2D selon la vitesse
	position += velocity * delta
	if is_touching:
		position.y -= 0.5

func _on_body_exited(_body):
	is_touching = false
	# (!) this will stop call _physics_process():
	set_physics_process(false)

func _on_timer_timeout():
	set_physics_process(true)

--- END OF FILE ---

--- FILE: /home/olivier/godotprojects/godot-prout-2d/scripts/dialog_bubble.gd ---
class_name TypewriterDisplay
extends Node2D

"""Displays text character by character with sound feedback.

Plays click sounds per character and return sounds on newlines.

Two modes controlled by wait_for_input:
- false (default): auto-hides after END_PAUSE. Original behavior.
- true: waits for try_advance() calls to progress or dismiss.

Supports multi-page sequences via show_pages().
"""

# --- Signals ---
signal page_finished()
signal all_pages_finished()

# --- Constants ---
const INTRO_DELAY: float = 0.51
const CHAR_DELAY: float = 0.06
const NEWLINE_DELAY: float = 0.7
const END_PAUSE: float = 1.0

# --- Exports ---
@export var sounds_click: Array[AudioStreamMP3] = []
@export var sounds_return: Array[AudioStreamMP3] = []
@export_multiline var text_to_display: String = "":
	set = _set_text_to_display
@export var wait_for_input: bool = false

# --- Private variables ---
var _is_waiting_end: bool = false
var _is_typing: bool = false
var _audio_players: Array[AudioStreamPlayer2D] = []
var _pages: Array[String] = []
var _current_page_index: int = 0

# --- Onready ---
@onready var _label: Label = (
	$VBoxContainer/MarginContainer/MarginContainerLabel/Label
)
@onready var _timer: Timer = $Timer
@onready var _animation_player: AnimationPlayer = $AnimationPlayer


# --- Built-in callbacks ---
func _ready() -> void:
	"""Initialize display state."""
	_label.text = ""
	visible = false


# --- Public methods ---
func show_pages(
	pages: Array[String], interactive: bool = true
) -> void:
	"""Start a multi-page dialog sequence.

	Args:
		pages: Array of strings, one per page.
		interactive: If true, waits for try_advance() between pages.
	"""
	if pages.is_empty():
		return
	_pages = pages
	_current_page_index = 0
	wait_for_input = interactive
	# Setting text_to_display triggers the setter which starts typing:
	text_to_display = _pages[0]


func try_advance() -> void:
	"""Advance the display when in wait_for_input mode.

	If still typing, skip to full text.
	If text fully shown, go to next page or dismiss.
	"""
	if not wait_for_input:
		return

	if _is_typing:
		# Skip to end of current page:
		_timer.stop()
		_label.text = text_to_display
		_is_typing = false
		_is_waiting_end = true
		return

	if _is_waiting_end:
		_is_waiting_end = false
		_advance_to_next_page()


func dismiss() -> void:
	"""Force-hide the bubble and reset state."""
	_timer.stop()
	_is_typing = false
	_is_waiting_end = false
	_pages = []
	_current_page_index = 0
	_animation_player.play("hide")


# --- Private methods ---
func _set_text_to_display(new_text: String) -> void:
	"""React to text_to_display being set.

	Assigning inside the setter does NOT re-trigger it in GDScript.

	Args:
		new_text: The full string to typewrite.
	"""
	if not is_node_ready():
		return

	text_to_display = new_text
	_label.text = ""
	_is_waiting_end = false
	_is_typing = true
	_animation_player.play("show")
	_timer.wait_time = INTRO_DELAY
	_timer.start()


func _advance_to_next_page() -> void:
	"""Move to the next page or finish if none left."""
	_current_page_index += 1
	if _current_page_index < _pages.size():
		page_finished.emit()
		# This triggers the setter which restarts typing:
		text_to_display = _pages[_current_page_index]
	else:
		_finish_all_pages()


func _on_timer_timeout() -> void:
	"""Advance the typewriter or trigger end behavior."""
	if _is_waiting_end:
		if wait_for_input:
			_timer.stop()
			return
		_timer.stop()
		_advance_to_next_page()
		return

	if _label.text.length() < text_to_display.length():
		_advance_typewriter()
	else:
		_is_typing = false
		_is_waiting_end = true
		if not wait_for_input:
			_timer.wait_time = END_PAUSE
			_timer.start()


func _advance_typewriter() -> void:
	"""Append the next character and schedule the following tick."""
	var next_index: int = _label.text.length()
	var ch: String = text_to_display.substr(next_index, 1)
	_label.text += ch

	if ch == "\n":
		play_rand_sound(sounds_return)
		_timer.wait_time = NEWLINE_DELAY
	else:
		play_rand_sound(sounds_click)
		_timer.wait_time = CHAR_DELAY

	_timer.start()


func _finish_all_pages() -> void:
	"""Hide the bubble and emit completion signal."""
	_pages = []
	_current_page_index = 0
	_animation_player.play("hide")
	all_pages_finished.emit()


func play_rand_sound(sounds: Array[AudioStreamMP3]) -> void:
	"""Play a random sound from the given array on an available player.

	Args:
		sounds: Pool of AudioStreamMP3 to pick from.
	"""
	if sounds.is_empty():
		return

	var player: AudioStreamPlayer2D = _get_available_player()
	player.stream = sounds[randi() % sounds.size()]
	player.play()


func _get_available_player() -> AudioStreamPlayer2D:
	"""Return a free AudioStreamPlayer2D, creating one if needed.

	Returns:
		An AudioStreamPlayer2D not currently playing.
	"""
	for player: AudioStreamPlayer2D in _audio_players:
		if not player.playing:
			return player

	var new_player := AudioStreamPlayer2D.new()
	add_child(new_player)
	_audio_players.append(new_player)
	return new_player


func _on_tree_exiting() -> void:
	sounds_click.clear()
	sounds_return.clear()

--- END OF FILE ---
